NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Commissioner  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
 
A. Mahendiran, a male child son of Thiru R. Arumugam, born on 24th March 1997 residing at Number 3/44, Vadapathi
Street, Sholampettai Post, Mayiladuthurai-609 003 as been living as female, I have been granted Identiry Card
Number NGI/006/2020 issued by Tamil Nadu Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department, by this,
I may be treated as female and shall henceforth be known as MIRTHULAMAHI.
Mayiladuthurai, 
A. MAHENDIRAN
3rd February 2021.
 
S. Vijayarajan, a male child born to Thiru G. Samynathan, born on 11th June 1991 residing at No. 86, Seeniyapuram
Street, Srivilliputhur, Virudhunagar-626 125, has been living as a female she has been granted an Identity Card No. 4812/09
issue by the Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfere and NMP Department. By this I may be treated
as a female and shall henceforth be known as S.VIJI
Virudhunagar, 
S. VIJAYARAJAN
3rd February 2021.
 
R. Aravindan, male Child, son of Thiru R. Ravi born on 27th December 1990 residing at No.13, Bajanai Kovil 
Street, Chitlapakkam, Hasthinapuram, Chennai-600 064, has been living as Female. I have been granted Identiry Card
No. 4663/09 issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and N.M.P. Department. By this I may be treated 
as female and shall henceforth be known as ASHWINI. R
Chennai, 
R. ARAVINDAN
3rd February 2021.
